msg:I recently had the pleasure of traveling to Rosewood Residence in GZ with my wife, and I must say, it was an exceptional experience.

Upon our slightly late check-in, we were warmly greeted by Doris, the receptionist. Her kindness was evident from the start, as she graciously upgraded us to a one-bedroom suite. This unexpected gesture set the tone for the rest of our stay.

What truly amazed us was the level of exclusivity and privacy offered at Rosewood Residence. The private elevator that led directly to our room was a delightful surprise. It enhanced our sense of luxury and seclusion, making us feel like we had our own private oasis. The absence of a traditional hallway meant that we couldn't hear any noise from outside, ensuring a peaceful and undisturbed stay.

As we stepped into our one-bedroom suite, we were captivated by the impeccable decor. The attention to detail and the luxurious ambiance made it feel like we were residing in a high-end condominium that exuded comfort and elegance. It truly felt like a home away from home.

Without a doubt, if we ever find ourselves back in GZ, we will not hesitate to return to Rosewood Residence. The exceptional service, the unrivaled exclusivity, and the remarkable attention to detail made our stay unforgettable. We highly recommend this extraordinary establishment to anyone seeking a truly exceptional and luxurious accommodation experience.

The rooms are relatively new.

Before coming to Guangzhou, I read a round of hotel reviews, and they all said that Rosewood‚Äôs service was very poor. Although I actually lived in the Rosewood Mansion, the actual check-in service was actually quite good. It‚Äôs just that these new employees don‚Äôt know how to deal with emergencies. The gym, swimming pool are shared with the Rosewood Hotel. In addition, the hotel cooperates with K11 (after all, they are all products of the Zheng family of the four major families in Hong Kong). I have to say that this wave of operations is very powerful.

When I checked out, I collected room cards with four different covers of the mansion, which satisfied my little desire for collection, and I was very happy.

Leaving aside some minor issues, in fact Rosewood is still a very beautiful and artistic hotel, otherwise why would you see so many beauties staying in the hotel? Perhaps it has something to do with the fact that the head of Magnificent Beauty is a woman. After all, who can understand women better than women, are you right?
